# AI ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤£‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å: ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∂‡≤ø

## ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤Ø

‡≤à ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø, ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å AI ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤£‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å (SLMs) ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤†‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤µ‡≥Å. ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç AI ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤§ ‡≤§‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, SLM ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ-‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å Microsoft ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤≥‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü.

‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§‡≤ï ‡≤¨‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤¶‡≥É‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≥Å 2025 ‡≤∞‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤≠‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü. 2023 ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤¨‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü, 2024 ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≤∞ ‡≤¨‡≥Ç‡≤Æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤§‡≥Å, 2025 AI ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‚Äî ‡≤¨‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ, ‡≤§‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ, ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ, ‡≤â‡≤™‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤† ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤µ ‡≤á‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ, ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤£‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§. Microsoft ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤à ‡≤¨‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤´‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤ñ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

## ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

‡≤à ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤ó, ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å:

- ü§ñ AI ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤§ ‡≤§‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
- üî¨ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤£‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤° ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤≤‡≥Ç ‡≤è‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤≠ ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
- üöÄ ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ SLM ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
- üì± ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü SLM-‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤†‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
- üèóÔ∏è Microsoft ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ-‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
- üåê ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø LLM ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å SLM ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤´‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
- üîß ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø Microsoft ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å Foundry Local ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å

## AI ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å: ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

### ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ñ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤§ ‡≤§‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§‡≤ï ‡≤¨‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ü (AI) ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤Ö‡≤•‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤•‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç, ‡≤§‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤â‡≤™‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï AI ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø, ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å.

### ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç

‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ó‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï:

- **üî¨ ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç**: ‡≤§‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤£‡≤¶ ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å (‡≤•‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤®‡≥Ü)
- **üì± ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç**: ‡≤Ü‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å (‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤¨‡≥ã‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç, ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å)
- **‚öñÔ∏è ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç**: ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤†‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å (‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥Å, ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤≥‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å)
- **üß† ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç**: ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤Ø‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å (‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤∏‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥Å)

### AI ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤ñ ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤≠‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

AI ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤π‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤§ ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤≠‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü:

**‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤§‡≥Ü**: ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤µ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï-‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤Ø ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü. ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤† ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤ó‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï‡≤∞.

**‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤§‡≥Ü**: ‡≤à ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤® AI ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤ó‡≥å‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤≠‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≥á‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥Ü.

**‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ**: ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥å‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤ó‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§.

## ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤£‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

### SLM (‡≤∏‡≤£‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø) ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤§‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

‡≤∏‡≤£‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø (SLM) ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ï ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤® ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤§‡≤°‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø. ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø, SLM ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø 10 ‡≤¨‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å.

**‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: SLM ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤, ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü, ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï-‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤Ø ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü. ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤ó‡≥å‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü WebGPU ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å.

**‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø SLM ‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤¨‡≥à‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤® ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥Å‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤§ Q4_K_M, ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤£‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü-‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü Q5_K_S ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ø, ‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤™‡≤¶ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ñ‡≤∞‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø Q8_0 ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥Ä ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç Q2_K ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥Ü.

### GGUF (‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤∞‡≤≤‡≥ç GGML ‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç) SLM ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü

GGUF CPU ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§ SLM ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥Å, ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü:

**‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç-‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤à ‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ü‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç, ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤î‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å-‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü SLM ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

**‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**: GGUF ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤£‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü, ‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å-‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤°‡≥à‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï-‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

### ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç-‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶ SLM ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

#### Llama.cpp ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç

Llama.cpp ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç SLM ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≥Å‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü:

**‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£**: ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç Q4_0 (75% ‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤¨‡≥à‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§), Q5_1 (‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤® ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤£‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü-‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥Å‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤§), ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å Q8_0 (‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥Ä‡≤™‡≤¶ ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤£‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü) ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ ‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤° ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥Å‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü.

**‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤†‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤≠‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: SIMD ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü CPU ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤ø-‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. x86, ARM ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

#### ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≤≤‡≥ç MLX ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø

‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≤≤‡≥ç MLX ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü SLM-‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü:

**‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**: ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤°‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü, ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ñ‡≤∞‡≤§‡≥Ü, ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å-‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥ç. M-‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≥ã‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü.

**‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∏ ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç API ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤, ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∏, ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø ‡≤â‡≤™‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü.

#### ONNX ‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ü‡≥à‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø

ONNX ‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ü‡≥à‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤Ø ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü:

**‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü**: ONNX ‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ü‡≥à‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥ç, ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç, ‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤é‡≤∏‡≥ç, iOS ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤ø‡≤∞ SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ñ‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤™‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤à ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤™‡≤°‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤í‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥Ü‡≤°‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∂ ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü, ‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å-‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≤æ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤π‡≤≥ ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

**‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç CPU (‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥Ü‡≤≤‡≥ç, AMD, ARM), GPU (NVIDIA CUDA, AMD ROCm), ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤∑ ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ï‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å (‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥Ü‡≤≤‡≥ç VPU, Qualcomm NPU) ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å.

**‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ-‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ONNX ‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ü‡≥à‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤¶ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤´‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç, ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü, ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ä‡≤´‡≥à‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤™‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤≥‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤ó‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥à‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å C++ API ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≤µ‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

## ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø SLM ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å LLM: ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ ‡≤π‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü

### ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø SLM ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤≠‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

**‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü**: SLM ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü LLM ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤§ 10-30√ó ‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ï‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ï-‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü. ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤ó‡≤£‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü.

**‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: SLM ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤≤‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤® ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶ ‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤ó‡≥å‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü, ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≥á‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å.

**‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**: SLM ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤ü‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç, ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤î‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞-‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤ï‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø (70-80% ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å) ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥Ü.

### ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø SLM ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å LLM ‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤∏‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤ï‡≥Å

**SLM ‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£**:
- **‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤®‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤°‡≥á‡≤ü‡≤æ ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø, ‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤≠‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø, ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø API ‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
- **‡≤ü‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£**: ‡≤°‡≥á‡≤ü‡≤æ‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤´‡≥à‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å, ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
- **‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
- **‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≥á‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç**: ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü, ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤≥‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø, ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥Ç‡≤§ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü
- **‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü**: ‡≤ó‡≥å‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü-‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

**LLM ‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ**:
- **‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤§‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï**: ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤∏ ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞, ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü
- **‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤¶ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç, ‡≤∏‡≥É‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ï ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
- **‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥É‡≤§ ‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤ú‡≥ç‡≤û‡≤æ‡≤® ‡≤Ö‡≤ó‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∂‡≥ã‡≤ß‡≤®‡≥Ü
- **‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤∏ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤∏ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤¶‡≥É‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å

### ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™

‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø SLM ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å LLM ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü:

**‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü**:
1. **SLM ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤•‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø**: 70-80% ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
2. **‡≤Ö‡≤µ‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤ó LLM**: ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥å‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤° ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∂‡≤® ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å
3. **‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤∑ SLM ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**: ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≥á‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤∏‡≤£‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
4. **‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**: ‡≤¨‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤∂‡≤®‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï ‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤¨‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø LLM ‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥Å

## ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

### Foundry Local: ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç AI ‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ü‡≥à‡≤Æ‡≥ç

Foundry Local (https://github.com/microsoft/foundry-local) ‡≤∏‡≤£‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤≠‡≤æ‡≤∑‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤≤‡≥Å Microsoft ‡≤® ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤ñ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü. ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å SLM-‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤∞‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ü‡≥à‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

**‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**:
- **OpenAI-‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤§ API**: OpenAI SDK ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü
- **‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**: ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç (CUDA GPU, Qualcomm NPU, CPU) ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤¨‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü
- **‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü**: SLM ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤°‡≥å‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç, ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ú‡≥Ä‡≤µ‡≤®‡≤ö‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü
- **‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∑‡≤£‡≥Ü**: ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∂‡≥Ç‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø-‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤™‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ü
- **‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**: ‡≤é‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç ‡≤¶‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤§‡≥Ü

#### ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç

**‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤®‡≥Ü**:
```bash
# ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥ç (‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤∏‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü)
winget install Microsoft.FoundryLocal

# ‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤í‡≤é‡≤∏‡≥ç
brew tap microsoft/foundrylocal
brew install foundrylocal

# ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏ (‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤®‡≥Ü)
wget https://github.com/microsoft/foundry-local/releases/latest/download/foundry-local-linux.tar.gz
tar -xzf foundry-local-linux.tar.gz
sudo mv foundry-local /usr/local/bin/
```

**‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠**:
```bash
# ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
foundry model run phi-4-mini

# ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
foundry service status

# ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
foundry model ls

# API ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
curl http://localhost:<port>/v1/models
```

#### ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£

**Foundry Local SDK ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£**:
```python
from foundry_local import FoundryLocalManager
from microsoft_agent_framework import Agent, Config
import openai

# Foundry Local ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
manager = FoundryLocalManager("phi-4-mini")

# ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø OpenAI ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
client = openai.OpenAI(
    base_url=manager.endpoint,
    api_key=manager.api_key  # ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç-‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤§
)

# Foundry Local ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
agent_config = Config(
    name="production-agent",
    model_provider="foundry-local",
    model_id=manager.get_model_info("phi-4-mini").id,
    endpoint=manager.endpoint,
    api_key=manager.api_key
)

agent = Agent(config=agent_config)
```

**‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**:
```python
# ‡≤´‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤Ø‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
models_by_use_case = {
    "lightweight_routing": "qwen2.5-0.5b",      # 500MB, ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø
    "general_conversation": "phi-4-mini",       # 2.4GB, ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤®
    "complex_reasoning": "phi-4",               # 7GB, ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø
    "code_assistance": "qwen2.5-coder-0.5b"    # 500MB, ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç-‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü
}

# ‡≤´‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
for use_case, model_alias in models_by_use_case.items():
    manager = FoundryLocalManager(model_alias)
    print(f"{use_case}: {manager.get_model_info(model_alias).variant_selected}")
    # ‡≤î‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å:
    # ‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ü‡≥ç_‡≤∞‡≥Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç: qwen2.5-0.5b-instruct-q4_k_m.gguf (CPU ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü)
    # ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø_‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶: phi-4-mini-instruct-cuda-q5_k_m.gguf (GPU ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤§)
```

#### ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

**‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç**:
```python
import asyncio
from foundry_local import FoundryLocalManager
from microsoft_agent_framework import Agent, Config, Tool

class ProductionAgentService:
    def __init__(self, model_alias="phi-4-mini"):
        self.foundry = FoundryLocalManager(model_alias)
        self.agent = self._create_agent()
        
    def _create_agent(self):
        config = Config(
            name="production-customer-service",
            model_provider="foundry-local",
            model_id=self.foundry.get_model_info().id,
            endpoint=self.foundry.endpoint,
            api_key=self.foundry.api_key,
            max_tokens=512,
            temperature=0.1,
            timeout=30.0
        )
        
        agent = Agent(config=config)
        
        # ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
        @agent.tool
        def lookup_customer(customer_id: str) -> dict:
            """Look up customer information from local database."""
            return self.local_db.get_customer(customer_id)
            
        @agent.tool
        def create_ticket(issue: str, priority: str = "medium") -> str:
            """Create a support ticket."""
            ticket_id = self.ticketing_system.create(issue, priority)
            return f"Created ticket {ticket_id}"
            
        return agent
    
    async def process_request(self, user_input: str) -> str:
        """Process user request with error handling and monitoring."""
        try:
            response = await self.agent.chat_async(user_input)
            self.log_interaction(user_input, response, "success")
            return response
        except Exception as e:
            self.log_interaction(user_input, str(e), "error")
            return "I'm experiencing technical difficulties. Please try again."
    
    def health_check(self) -> dict:
        """Check service health for monitoring."""
        return {
            "foundry_status": self.foundry.health_check(),
            "model_loaded": self.foundry.is_model_loaded(),
            "endpoint": self.foundry.endpoint,
            "memory_usage": self.foundry.get_memory_usage()
        }

# ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü
service = ProductionAgentService("phi-4-mini")
response = await service.process_request("I need help with my order #12345")
```

**‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å-‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü**:
```python
from foundry_local import FoundryLocalManager
from microsoft_agent_framework import AgentOrchestrator, Agent, Config

class MultiAgentProductionSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.agents = self._initialize_agents()
        self.orchestrator = AgentOrchestrator(list(self.agents.values()))
        
    def _initialize_agents(self):
        agents = {}
        
        # ‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç
        routing_foundry = FoundryLocalManager("qwen2.5-0.5b")
        agents["router"] = Agent(Config(
            name="request-router",
            model_provider="foundry-local",
            endpoint=routing_foundry.endpoint,
            api_key=routing_foundry.api_key,
            role="Route user requests to appropriate specialized agents"
        ))
        
        # ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç
        service_foundry = FoundryLocalManager("phi-4-mini")
        agents["customer_service"] = Agent(Config(
            name="customer-service",
            model_provider="foundry-local",
            endpoint=service_foundry.endpoint,
            api_key=service_foundry.api_key,
            role="Handle customer service inquiries and support requests"
        ))
        
        # ‡≤§‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ï ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç
        tech_foundry = FoundryLocalManager("qwen2.5-coder-0.5b")
        agents["technical"] = Agent(Config(
            name="technical-support",
            model_provider="foundry-local",
            endpoint=tech_foundry.endpoint,
            api_key=tech_foundry.api_key,
            role="Provide technical assistance and troubleshooting"
        ))
        
        return agents
    
    async def process_request(self, user_input: str) -> str:
        """Route and process user requests through appropriate agents."""
        # ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
        routing_result = await self.agents["router"].chat_async(
            f"Classify this request and route to customer_service or technical: {user_input}"
        )
        
        # ‡≤∞‡≥å‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü ‡≤ó‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
        target_agent = "customer_service" if "customer" in routing_result.lower() else "technical"
        
        # ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤∑‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
        response = await self.agents[target_agent].chat_async(user_input)
        
        return response

# ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü
system = MultiAgentProductionSystem()
response = await system.process_request("My application keeps crashing")
```

#### ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü

**‡≤Ü‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ó‡≤Æ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤π‡≤§‡≥Ü**:
```python
from foundry_local import FoundryLocalManager
import asyncio
import logging

class FoundryMonitoringService:
    def __init__(self):
        self.managers = {}
        self.metrics = []
        
    def add_model(self, alias: str) -> FoundryLocalManager:
        """Add a model to monitoring."""
        manager = FoundryLocalManager(alias)
        self.managers[alias] = manager
        return manager
    
    async def collect_metrics(self):
        """Collect performance metrics from all Foundry Local instances."""
        metrics = {
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "models": {}
        }
        
        for alias, manager in self.managers.items():
            try:
                model_metrics = {
                    "status": "healthy" if manager.health_check() else "unhealthy",
                    "memory_usage": manager.get_memory_usage(),
                    "inference_count": manager.get_inference_count(),
                    "average_latency": manager.get_average_latency(),
                    "error_rate": manager.get_error_rate()
                }
                metrics["models"][alias] = model_metrics
            except Exception as e:
                logging.error(f"Failed to collect metrics for {alias}: {e}")
                metrics["models"][alias] = {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}
        
        self.metrics.append(metrics)
        return metrics
    
    def get_health_status(self) -> dict:
        """Get overall system health status."""
        healthy_models = 0
        total_models = len(self.managers)
        
        for alias, manager in self.managers.items():
            if manager.health_check():
                healthy_models += 1
        
        return {
            "overall_status": "healthy" if healthy_models == total_models else "degraded",
            "healthy_models": healthy_models,
            "total_models": total_models,
            "health_percentage": (healthy_models / total_models) * 100 if total_models > 0 else 0
        }

# ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤æ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü
monitor = FoundryMonitoringService()
monitor.add_model("phi-4-mini")
monitor.add_model("qwen2.5-0.5b")

# ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü
async def monitoring_loop():
    while True:
        metrics = await monitor.collect_metrics()
        health = monitor.get_health_status()
        
        if health["health_percentage"] < 100:
            logging.warning(f"System health degraded: {health}")
        
        await asyncio.sleep(30)  # ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø 30 ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤≥‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
```

**‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç-‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç**:
```python
class FoundryResourceManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model_instances = {}
        self.resource_limits = {
            "max_memory_gb": 8,
            "max_concurrent_models": 3,
            "cpu_threshold": 80
        }
    
    def auto_scale_models(self, demand_metrics: dict):
        """Automatically scale models based on demand."""
        current_memory = self.get_total_memory_usage()
        
        # ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤°‡≥å‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
        if current_memory > self.resource_limits["max_memory_gb"] * 0.8:
            self.scale_down_idle_models()
        
        # ‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥Ü‡≤ö‡≥ç‡≤ö‡≥Å ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
        for model_alias, demand in demand_metrics.items():
            if demand > 0.8 and len(self.model_instances) < self.resource_limits["max_concurrent_models"]:
                self.load_model_instance(model_alias)
    
    def load_model_instance(self, alias: str) -> FoundryLocalManager:
        """Load a new model instance if resources allow."""
        if alias not in self.model_instances:
            try:
                manager = FoundryLocalManager(alias)
                self.model_instances[alias] = manager
                logging.info(f"Loaded model instance: {alias}")
                return manager
            except Exception as e:
                logging.error(f"Failed to load model {alias}: {e}")
                return None
        return self.model_instances[alias]
    
    def scale_down_idle_models(self):
        """Remove idle model instances to free resources."""
        idle_models = []
        
        for alias, manager in self.model_instances.items():
            if manager.get_idle_time() > 300:  # 5 ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ú‡≤®‡≤§‡≥Ü
                idle_models.append(alias)
        
        for alias in idle_models:
            self.model_instances[alias].shutdown()
            del self.model_instances[alias]
            logging.info(f"Scaled down idle model: {alias}")
```

#### ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç

**‡≤ï‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü**:
```python
# ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü
from foundry_local import FoundryLocalManager, ModelConfig

# ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü
config = ModelConfig(
    alias="phi-4-mini",
    quantization="Q5_K_M",  # ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü
    context_length=4096,    # ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥É‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤≠
    batch_size=1,          # ‡≤è‡≤ï-‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü
    threads=4,             # CPU ‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç
    gpu_layers=32,         # GPU ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
    memory_lock=True,      # ‡≤∏‡≤§‡≤§ ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
    numa=True              # ‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å-‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø NUMA ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç
)

manager = FoundryLocalManager(config=config)
```

**‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤™‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø**:

‚úÖ **‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü**:
- ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤æ ‡≤ó‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤Ü‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤´‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

‚úÖ **‡≤≠‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç**:
- ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø-‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ API ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø (‡≤¨‡≤æ‡≤π‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶‡≥Ü)
- ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ API ‡≤ï‡≥Ä ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Ü‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤¶‡≤∞ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≥Ç‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

‚úÖ **‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**:
- ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤Æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å CPU ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

‚úÖ **‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≥Ü**:
- ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤Ü‡≤´‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤´‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤®‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞ ‡≤¶‡≥É‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø-‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤¶-‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

### Ollama: ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§ SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü

### Ollama: ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø-‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§ SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü

Ollama ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥‡≤§‡≥Ü, ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ï ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤™‡≤°‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï‡≤∞ ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü ‡≤í‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤®‡≥Ä‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ SLM ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤®‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤í‡≤¶‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü. Foundry Local ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≥á‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó, Ollama ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ü‡≥à‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç, ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤¶‡≥É‡≤∂‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤Æ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü.

**‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤™ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å**:
- **OpenAI-‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤§ API**: ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤∞ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤£ REST API ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤£‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü
- **‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ï ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤Ø**: ‡≤®‡≥Ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥É‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂
- **‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤≥ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü**: ‡≤í‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥á ‡≤ï‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≤£‡≥Ü
- **‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤**: ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥ç, ‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ã‡≤é‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤¨‡≤≤
- **‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**: ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤£‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ü

#### ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç

**‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≥ç-‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤®‡≥Ü**:
```bash
# ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥ç
winget install Ollama.Ollama

# ‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤í‡≤é‡≤∏‡≥ç
brew install ollama

# ‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏
curl -fsSL https://ollama.com/install.sh | sh

# ‡≤°‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü
docker run -d -v ollama:/root/.ollama -p 11434:11434 --name ollama ollama/ollama
```

**‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠**:
```bash
# ‡≤í‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
ollama serve

# ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤°‡≥å‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
ollama pull phi3.5:3.8b-mini-instruct-q4_K_M    # ‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥à-3.5 ‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤ø
ollama pull qwen2.5:0.5b-instruct-q4_K_M        # ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤®‡≥ç2.5 0.5‡≤¨‡≤ø
ollama pull llama3.2:1b-instruct-q4_K_M         # ‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ 3.2 1‡≤¨‡≤ø

# ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
ollama list

# API ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
curl http://localhost:11434/api/generate -d '{
  "model": "phi3.5:3.8b-mini-instruct-q4_K_M",
  "prompt": "Hello, how can I help you today?"
}'
```

#### ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£

**Microsoft ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü Ollama**:
```python
from microsoft_agent_framework import Agent, Config
import openai
import requests
import json

class OllamaManager:
    def __init__(self, model_name: str, base_url: str = "http://localhost:11434"):
        self.model_name = model_name
        self.base_url = base_url
        self.api_url = f"{base_url}/api"
        self.openai_url = f"{base_url}/v1"
        
    def ensure_model_available(self) -> bool:
        """Ensure the model is pulled and available."""
        try:
            response = requests.post(f"{self.api_url}/pull", 
                json={"name": self.model_name})
            return response.status_code == 200
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to pull model {self.model_name}: {e}")
            return False
    
    def get_openai_client(self) -> openai.OpenAI:
        """Get OpenAI-compatible client for Ollama."""
        return openai.OpenAI(
            base_url=self.openai_url,
            api_key="ollama",  # ‡≤í‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ú‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶ API ‡≤ï‡≥Ä ‡≤Ö‡≤ó‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤
        )
    
    def health_check(self) -> bool:
        """Check if Ollama service is running."""
        try:
            response = requests.get(f"{self.base_url}/api/tags")
            return response.status_code == 200
        except:
            return False

# ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤í‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
ollama_manager = OllamaManager("phi3.5:3.8b-mini-instruct-q4_K_M")
ollama_manager.ensure_model_available()

# ‡≤í‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ ‡≤¨‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤®‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
agent_config = Config(
    name="ollama-agent",
    model_provider="ollama",
    model_id="phi3.5:3.8b-mini-instruct-q4_K_M",
    endpoint=ollama_manager.openai_url,
    api_key="ollama"
)

agent = Agent(config=agent_config)
```

**Ollama ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≤π‡≥Å-‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç**:
```python
class OllamaMultiModelManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.models = {
            "lightweight": "qwen2.5:0.5b-instruct-q4_K_M",      # 350MB
            "balanced": "phi3.5:3.8b-mini-instruct-q4_K_M",     # 2.3GB
            "capable": "llama3.2:3b-instruct-q4_K_M",           # 1.9GB
            "coding": "codellama:7b-code-q4_K_M"                # 4.1GB
        }
        self.base_url = "http://localhost:11434"
        self.clients = {}
        self._initialize_models()
    
    def _initialize_models(self):
        """Pull all required models and create clients."""
        for category, model_name in self.models.items():
            # ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≤¶‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤ø
            self._pull_model(model_name)
            
            # ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø OpenAI ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
            self.clients[category] = openai.OpenAI(
                base_url=f"{self.base_url}/v1",
                api_key="ollama"
            )
    
    def _pull_model(self, model_name: str):
        """Pull model if not already available."""
        try:
            response = requests.post(f"{self.base_url}/api/pull", 
                json={"name": model_name})
            if response.status_code == 200:
                print(f"Model {model_name} ready")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to pull {model_name}: {e}")
    
    def get_agent_for_task(self, task_type: str) -> Agent:
        """Get appropriate agent based on task complexity."""
        model_category = self._classify_task(task_type)
        model_name = self.models[model_category]
        
        config = Config(
            name=f"ollama-{model_category}-agent",
            model_provider="ollama",
            model_id=model_name,
            endpoint=f"{self.base_url}/v1",
            api_key="ollama"
        )
        
        return Agent(config=config)
    
    def _classify_task(self, task_type: str) -> str:
        """Classify task to appropriate model category."""
        if any(keyword in task_type.lower() for keyword in ["simple", "route", "classify"]):
            return "lightweight"
        elif any(keyword in task_type.lower() for keyword in ["code", "programming", "debug"]):
            return "coding"
        elif any(keyword in task_type.lower() for keyword in ["complex", "analysis", "research"]):
            return "capable"
        else:
            return "balanced"

# ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü
manager = OllamaMultiModelManager()

# ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤® ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø
routing_agent = manager.get_agent_for_task("simple routing")
coding_agent = manager.get_agent_for_task("code debugging")
analysis_agent = manager.get_agent_for_task("complex analysis")
```

#### ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å

**Ollama ‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤‡≤ï ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü**:
```python
import asyncio
import logging
from typing import Dict, Optional
from microsoft_agent_framework import Agent, Config
import requests
import openai

class OllamaProductionService:
    def __init__(self, models_config: Dict[str, str]):
        self.models_config = models_config
        self.base_url = "http://localhost:11434"
        self.agents = {}
        self.metrics = {
            "requests_processed": 0,
            "errors": 0,
            "model_usage": {model: 0 for model in models_config.keys()}
        }
        self._initialize_production_agents()
    
    def _initialize_production_agents(self):
        """Initialize production agents with health checks."""
        for agent_type, model_name in self.models_config.items():
            try:
                # ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤ñ‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤™‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≥ç‡≤≥‡≤ø
                self._ensure_model_ready(model_name)
                
                # ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
                config = Config(
                    name=f"production-{agent_type}",
                    model_provider="ollama",
                    model_id=model_name,
                    endpoint=f"{self.base_url}/v1",
                    api_key="ollama",
                    max_tokens=512,
                    temperature=0.1,
                    timeout=30.0
                )
                
                agent = Agent(config=config)
                
                # ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤¶ ‡≤Ü‡≤ß‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥Ü ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤ß‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
                self._add_production_tools(agent, agent_type)
                
                self.agents[agent_type] = agent
                logging.info(f"Initialized {agent_type} agent with model {model_name}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                logging.error(f"Failed to initialize {agent_type} agent: {e}")
    
    def _ensure_model_ready(self, model_name: str):
        """Ensure model is pulled and ready for use."""
        try:
            # ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤Ö‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤¶‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥á ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
            response = requests.get(f"{self.base_url}/api/tags")
            models = response.json().get('models', [])
            
            model_exists = any(model['name'] == model_name for model in models)
            
            if not model_exists:
                logging.info(f"Pulling model {model_name}...")
                pull_response = requests.post(f"{self.base_url}/api/pull", 
                    json={"name": model_name})
                
                if pull_response.status_code != 200:
                    raise Exception(f"Failed to pull model {model_name}")
                    
        except Exception as e:
            raise Exception(f"Model setup failed for {model_name}: {e}")
    
    def _add_production_tools(self, agent: Agent, agent_type: str):
        """Add tools based on agent type."""
        if agent_type == "customer_service":
            @agent.tool
            def lookup_customer(customer_id: str) -> dict:
                """Look up customer information."""
                # ‡≤°‡≥á‡≤ü‡≤æ‡≤¨‡≥á‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤π‡≥Å‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ü‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
                return {"customer_id": customer_id, "status": "active", "tier": "premium"}
            
            @agent.tool
            def create_support_ticket(issue: str, priority: str = "medium") -> str:
                """Create a support ticket."""
                ticket_id = f"TICK-{hash(issue) % 10000:04d}"
                return f"Created ticket {ticket_id} with priority {priority}"
        
        elif agent_type == "technical_support":
            @agent.tool
            def run_diagnostics(system_info: str) -> dict:
                """Run system diagnostics."""
                return {"status": "healthy", "issues": [], "recommendations": []}
            
            @agent.tool
            def access_knowledge_base(query: str) -> str:
                """Search technical knowledge base."""
                return f"Knowledge base results for: {query}"
    
    async def process_request(self, request: str, agent_type: str = "customer_service") -> dict:
        """Process user request with monitoring and error handling."""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        try:
            if agent_type not in self.agents:
                raise ValueError(f"Agent type {agent_type} not available")
            
            agent = self.agents[agent_type]
            response = await agent.chat_async(request)
            
            # ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤µ‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
            self.metrics["requests_processed"] += 1
            self.metrics["model_usage"][agent_type] += 1
            
            processing_time = time.time() - start_time
            
            self._log_interaction(request, response, "success", processing_time, agent_type)
            
            return {
                "response": response,
                "status": "success",
                "processing_time": processing_time,
                "agent_type": agent_type
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.metrics["errors"] += 1
            processing_time = time.time() - start_time
            
            self._log_interaction(request, str(e), "error", processing_time, agent_type)
            
            return {
                "response": "I'm experiencing technical difficulties. Please try again.",
                "status": "error",
                "error": str(e),
                "processing_time": processing_time
            }
    
    def _log_interaction(self, request: str, response: str, status: str, 
                        processing_time: float, agent_type: str):
        """Log interaction for monitoring and analysis."""
        logging.info(f"Agent: {agent_type}, Status: {status}, Time: {processing_time:.2f}s")
        
        # ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø, ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤¨‡≤∞‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
        log_entry = {
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "agent_type": agent_type,
            "request_length": len(request),
            "response_length": len(response),
            "status": status,
            "processing_time": processing_time
        }
    
    def get_health_status(self) -> dict:
        """Get service health status."""
        try:
            # ‡≤í‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤Ü‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
            response = requests.get(f"{self.base_url}/api/tags", timeout=5)
            ollama_healthy = response.status_code == 200
            
            # ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
            available_models = []
            if ollama_healthy:
                models = response.json().get('models', [])
                available_models = [model['name'] for model in models]
            
            return {
                "service_status": "healthy" if ollama_healthy else "unhealthy",
                "ollama_endpoint": self.base_url,
                "available_models": available_models,
                "active_agents": list(self.agents.keys()),
                "metrics": self.metrics,
                "timestamp": time.time()
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            return {
                "service_status": "error",
                "error": str(e),
                "timestamp": time.time()
            }

# ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü
production_models = {
    "customer_service": "phi3.5:3.8b-mini-instruct-q4_K_M",
    "technical_support": "llama3.2:3b-instruct-q4_K_M",
    "routing": "qwen2.5:0.5b-instruct-q4_K_M"
}

service = OllamaProductionService(production_models)

# ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤®‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
result = await service.process_request(
    "I need help with my account settings", 
    "customer_service"
)
print(result)
```

#### ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü

**Ollama ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ó‡≤Æ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤π‡≤§‡≥Ü**:
```python
import time
import asyncio
import requests
from typing import Dict, List

class OllamaMonitoringService:
    def __init__(self, base_url: str = "http://localhost:11434"):
        self.base_url = base_url
        self.metrics_history = []
        self.alert_thresholds = {
            "response_time_ms": 2000,
            "error_rate_percent": 5,
            "memory_usage_percent": 85
        }
    
    async def collect_metrics(self) -> dict:
        """Collect comprehensive metrics from Ollama service."""
        metrics = {
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "service_status": "unknown",
            "models": {},
            "performance": {},
            "resources": {}
        }
        
        try:
            # ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤Ü‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
            health_response = requests.get(f"{self.base_url}/api/tags", timeout=5)
            metrics["service_status"] = "healthy" if health_response.status_code == 200 else "unhealthy"
            
            if metrics["service_status"] == "healthy":
                # ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø
                models_data = health_response.json().get('models', [])
                for model in models_data:
                    model_name = model['name']
                    metrics["models"][model_name] = {
                        "size_gb": model.get('size', 0) / (1024**3),
                        "modified": model.get('modified_at', ''),
                        "digest": model.get('digest', '')[:12]  # ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤∂
                    }
                
                # ‡≤ä‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤™‡≥ã‡≤π‡≤¶ ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
                start_time = time.time()
                test_response = requests.post(f"{self.base_url}/api/generate", 
                    json={
                        "model": list(metrics["models"].keys())[0] if metrics["models"] else "",
                        "prompt": "Hello",
                        "stream": False
                    }, timeout=10)
                
                if test_response.status_code == 200:
                    inference_time = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                    metrics["performance"] = {
                        "inference_time_ms": inference_time,
                        "tokens_per_second": self._calculate_tokens_per_second(test_response.json()),
                        "last_successful_inference": time.time()
                    }
            
        except Exception as e:
            metrics["service_status"] = "error"
            metrics["error"] = str(e)
        
        self.metrics_history.append(metrics)
        
        # ‡≤ï‡≥ä‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø 100 ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤á‡≤°‡≤ø
        if len(self.metrics_history) > 100:
            self.metrics_history = self.metrics_history[-100:]
        
        return metrics
    
    def _calculate_tokens_per_second(self, response_data: dict) -> float:
        """Calculate approximate tokens per second from response."""
        try:
            # ‡≤ü‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤ú‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø (‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤ú‡≥Å)
            response_text = response_data.get('response', '')
            estimated_tokens = len(response_text.split())
            
            # ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤Ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤π‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≤ø
            eval_duration = response_data.get('eval_duration', 0)
            if eval_duration > 0:
                # ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
                duration_seconds = eval_duration / 1e9
                return estimated_tokens / duration_seconds if duration_seconds > 0 else 0
        except:
            pass
        return 0
    
    def check_alerts(self, current_metrics: dict) -> List[dict]:
        """Check current metrics against alert thresholds."""
        alerts = []
        
        # ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
        if current_metrics.get('performance', {}).get('inference_time_ms', 0) > self.alert_thresholds['response_time_ms']:
            alerts.append({
                "type": "performance",
                "message": f"High response time: {current_metrics['performance']['inference_time_ms']:.0f}ms",
                "severity": "warning"
            })
        
        # ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ø ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤ø‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
        if current_metrics.get('service_status') != 'healthy':
            alerts.append({
                "type": "availability",
                "message": f"Service unhealthy: {current_metrics.get('error', 'Unknown error')}",
                "severity": "critical"
            })
        
        return alerts
    
    def get_performance_summary(self, minutes: int = 60) -> dict:
        """Get performance summary for the last N minutes."""
        cutoff_time = time.time() - (minutes * 60)
        recent_metrics = [m for m in self.metrics_history if m['timestamp'] > cutoff_time]
        
        if not recent_metrics:
            return {"error": "No recent metrics available"}
        
        # ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
        response_times = [m.get('performance', {}).get('inference_time_ms', 0) 
                         for m in recent_metrics if m.get('performance')]
        
        healthy_checks = sum(1 for m in recent_metrics if m.get('service_status') == 'healthy')
        uptime_percent = (healthy_checks / len(recent_metrics)) * 100 if recent_metrics else 0
        
        return {
            "period_minutes": minutes,
            "total_checks": len(recent_metrics),
            "uptime_percent": uptime_percent,
            "avg_response_time_ms": sum(response_times) / len(response_times) if response_times else 0,
            "max_response_time_ms": max(response_times) if response_times else 0,
            "min_response_time_ms": min(response_times) if response_times else 0
        }

# ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤æ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü
monitor = OllamaMonitoringService()

async def monitoring_loop():
    """Continuous monitoring loop."""
    while True:
        try:
            metrics = await monitor.collect_metrics()
            alerts = monitor.check_alerts(metrics)
            
            if alerts:
                for alert in alerts:
                    logging.warning(f"ALERT: {alert['message']} (Severity: {alert['severity']})")
            
            # ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø 10 ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤Ç‡≤∂‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
            if int(time.time()) % 600 == 0:  # ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø 10 ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥Ü
                summary = monitor.get_performance_summary(10)
                logging.info(f"Performance Summary: {summary}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Monitoring error: {e}")
        
        await asyncio.sleep(30)  # ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø 30 ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

# ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
# asyncio.create_task(monitoring_loop())
```

#### ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç

**Ollama ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤ï‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤Æ‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü**:
```python
class OllamaModelManager:
    def __init__(self, base_url: str = "http://localhost:11434"):
        self.base_url = base_url
        self.model_catalog = {
            # ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
            "ultra_light": [
                "qwen2.5:0.5b-instruct-q4_K_M",
                "tinyllama:1.1b-chat-q4_K_M"
            ],
            # ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
            "balanced": [
                "phi3.5:3.8b-mini-instruct-q4_K_M",
                "llama3.2:3b-instruct-q4_K_M"
            ],
            # ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥á‡≤∑ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
            "code_specialist": [
                "codellama:7b-code-q4_K_M",
                "codegemma:7b-code-q4_K_M"
            ],
            # ‡≤â‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤§ ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤¶ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å
            "high_capability": [
                "llama3.1:8b-instruct-q4_K_M",
                "qwen2.5:7b-instruct-q4_K_M"
            ]
        }
    
    def setup_production_models(self, categories: List[str]) -> dict:
        """Set up models for production use."""
        setup_results = {}
        
        for category in categories:
            if category not in self.model_catalog:
                setup_results[category] = {"status": "error", "message": "Unknown category"}
                continue
            
            models = self.model_catalog[category]
            category_results = []
            
            for model in models:
                try:
                    # ‡≤™‡≥Å‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø
                    response = requests.post(f"{self.base_url}/api/pull", 
                        json={"name": model})
                    
                    if response.status_code == 200:
                        category_results.append({"model": model, "status": "ready"})
                    else:
                        category_results.append({"model": model, "status": "failed"})
                        
                except Exception as e:
                    category_results.append({"model": model, "status": "error", "error": str(e)})
            
            setup_results[category] = category_results
        
        return setup_results
    
    def optimize_for_hardware(self) -> dict:
        """Recommend optimal models based on available hardware."""
        # ‡≤á‡≤¶‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤ú‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤™‡≥Ü‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤¶‡≥Ü
        # ‡≤°‡≥Ü‡≤Æ‡≥ä ‡≤â‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü, ‡≤®‡≤æ‡≤µ‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≥Å‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥Å‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤µ‡≥Å
        
        recommendations = {
            "low_resource": {
                "models": ["qwen2.5:0.5b-instruct-q4_K_M"],
                "max_concurrent": 1,
                "memory_usage": "< 1GB"
            },
            "medium_resource": {
                "models": ["phi3.5:3.8b-mini-instruct-q4_K_M", "llama3.2:3b-instruct-q4_K_M"],
                "max_concurrent": 2,
                "memory_usage": "2-4GB"
            },
            "high_resource": {
                "models": ["llama3.1:8b-instruct-q4_K_M", "codellama:7b-code-q4_K_M"],
                "max_concurrent": 3,
                "memory_usage": "6-12GB"
            }
        }
        
        return recommendations

# ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç
model_manager = OllamaModelManager()
setup_results = model_manager.setup_production_models(["balanced", "ultra_light"])
print(f"Model setup results: {setup_results}")
```

**Ollama ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥ã‡≤ú‡≤®‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤®‡≤æ ‡≤™‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø**:

‚úÖ **‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤®‡≥Ü**:
- ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥Ü ‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤¶‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü Ollama ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤∏‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤¶ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤Ç‡≤≠ ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥á‡≤µ‡≥Ü ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤π‡≥ä‡≤Ç‡≤¶‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å API ‡≤≤‡≤≠‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

‚úÖ **‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü**:
- ‡≤Ö‡≤ó‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Å‡≤µ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤°‡≥å‡≤®‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤Ö‡≤ñ‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤®‡≤µ‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤ü‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤£‡≤æ ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤Ö‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

‚úÖ **‡≤≠‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤§‡≤æ ‡≤∏‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤Ö‡≤™‡≥ç**:
- ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤≥‡≥Ä‡≤Ø-‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞ ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤´‡≥à‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Æ‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- API ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤¶‡≤∞ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤Ø‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤®‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø ‡≤Ü‡≤°‡≤ø‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤ó‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤ú‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü‡≥Ç‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤∏‡≥Å‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤µ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

‚úÖ **‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Ü‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤∑‡≤®‡≥ç**:
- ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤§ ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤¨‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ö‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø
- ‡≤∏‡≥Ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤§ ‡≤π‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤°‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤ó‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤®‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤∞‡≤ö‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤µ‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤Ç‡≤ó‡≥ç ‡≤§‡≤Ç‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≥ç‡≤•‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø
- ‡≤∏‡≤Ç‡≤™‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Æ‡≥Ç‡≤≤ ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≥Ü‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤ø‡≤ö‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø

‚úÖ **‡≤è‡≤ï‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£ ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≥Ü**:
- ‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤Æ‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç ‡≤á‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤ø‡≤ó‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≥Ü ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤°‡≤ø  
- ‡≤Ü‡≤´‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤≤‡≥à‡≤®‡≥ç ‡≤ï‡≤æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤ö‡≤∞‡≤£‡≥Ü ‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤•‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∂‡≥Ä‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø  
- ‡≤´‡≥á‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤ì‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç ‡≤∏‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤¶‡≥ã‡≤∑ ‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤µ‡≤π‡≤£‡≥Ü‡≤Ø‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≥Ä‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø  
- ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç-‡≤ü‡≥Å-‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç ‡≤è‡≤ú‡≥Ü‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≥ç ‡≤µ‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤ï‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤ó‡≤≥‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤®‡≥Å ‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤®‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤ó‡≥ä‡≤≥‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤ø  

**‡≤´‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç ‡≤ú‡≥ä‡≤§‡≥Ü‡≤ó‡≥Ü ‡≤π‡≥ã‡≤≤‡≤ø‡≤ï‡≥Ü**:

| ‡≤µ‡≥à‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç‡≤Ø | ‡≤´‡≥å‡≤Ç‡≤°‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤≤‡≥ã‡≤ï‡≤≤‡≥ç | ‡≤í‡≤≤‡≥ç‡≤≤‡≤æ‡≤Æ‡≤æ |
|---------|---------------|--------|
| **‡≤≤‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∑‡≥ç‡≤Ø ‡≤¨‡≤≥‡≤ï‡≥Ü ‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≤ï‡≤∞‡≤£** | ‡≤é‡≤Ç‡≤ü‡≤∞‡≥ç‚Äå‡≤™‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥à‡≤∏‡≥ç ‡≤â‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤™‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤®‡≥Ü | ‡≤Ö‡≤≠‡≤ø‡≤µ‡≥É‡≤¶‡≥ç‡≤ß‡≤ø ‡≤Æ‡≤§‡≥ç‡≤§‡≥Å ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø |
| **‡≤Æ‡≤æ‡≤¶‡≤∞‡≤ø ‡≤™‡≤∞‡≤ø‡≤∏‡≤∞** | ‡≤Æ‡≥à‡≤ï‡≥ç‡≤∞‡≥ã‡≤∏‡≤æ‡≤´‡≥ç‡≤ü‡≥ç-‡≤®‡≤ø‡≤∞‡≥ç‡≤¶‡≥á‡≤∂‡≤ø‡≤§ | ‡≤µ‡≥ç‡≤Ø‡≤æ‡≤™‡≤ï ‡≤∏‡≤Æ‡≥Å‡≤¶‡≤æ‡≤Ø |
